029052:     function toggleFeature(feature) {
029053:         if (feature === 'clean') state.cleanMode = !state.cleanMode;
029054:         if (feature === 'markerFocus') state.markerFocus = !state.markerFocus;
029055:         if (feature === 'missionPulse') state.missionPulse = !state.missionPulse;
029056:         if (feature === 'roadPriority') state.roadPriority = !state.roadPriority;
029057:         if (feature === 'coverage') state.coverage.enabled = !state.coverage.enabled;
029058:         if (feature === 'heatmap') state.heatmap.enabled = !state.heatmap.enabled;
029059:         if (feature === 'shortcuts') state.shortcuts = !state.shortcuts;
029060:         if (feature === 'autoLoadAllVehicles') {
029061:             state.autoLoadAllVehicles = !state.autoLoadAllVehicles;
029062:             if (state.autoLoadAllVehicles) installAutoLoadAllVehicles();
029063:             else stopAutoLoadAllVehicles();
029064:         }
029065:         if (feature === 'allianceBuildingsMapBlocker') state.allianceBuildingsMap = state.allianceBuildingsMap === false;
029066:         if (feature === 'majorIncidentFeed') state.majorIncidentFeed.enabled = !state.majorIncidentFeed.enabled;
029067:         if (feature === 'missionLockAudio') {
029068:             state.missionLockAudio = !state.missionLockAudio;
029069:             if (state.missionLockAudio) unlockPayoutAudio(true);
029070:         }
029071:         if (feature === 'allianceCredits') state.allianceCredits = !state.allianceCredits;
029072:         if (feature === 'missionAge') state.missionAge = !state.missionAge;
029073:         if (feature === 'unitCommitment') state.unitCommitment = !state.unitCommitment;
029074:         if (feature === 'transportWatcher') state.transportWatcher = !state.transportWatcher;

029170: 
029171:     function runAutoNight(force = false) {
029172:         if (!state.autoNight.enabled) return;
029173:         const bucket = isNightNow(state.autoNight.nightStart, state.autoNight.dayStart) ? 'night' : 'day';
029174:         if (!force && state.autoNight.lastBucket === bucket) return;
029175:         state.autoNight.lastBucket = bucket;
029176:         state.theme = bucket === 'night' ? normaliseTheme(state.autoNight.nightTheme) : normaliseTheme(state.autoNight.dayTheme);
029177:         saveState();
029178:         applyRootAttributes();
029179:         updateUI();
029180:     }
029181: 
029182:     function isNightNow(start, end) {
029183:         const now = new Date();
029184:         const current = now.getHours() * 60 + now.getMinutes();
029185:         const startMin = parseTime(start, 19 * 60);
029186:         const endMin = parseTime(end, 7 * 60);
029187:         if (startMin === endMin) return false;
029188:         if (startMin < endMin) return current >= startMin && current < endMin;
029189:         return current >= startMin || current < endMin;
029190:     }
029191: 
029192:     function parseTime(value, fallback) {
029193:         const match = String(value || '').match(/^(\d{1,2}):(\d{2})$/);
029194:         if (!match) return fallback;
029195:         return clamp(match[1], 0, 23, Math.floor(fallback / 60)) * 60 + clamp(match[2], 0, 59, fallback % 60);
029196:     }
029197: 
029198:     function shouldSuppressControl() {
029199:         if (state.cleanMode) return false;
029200:         if (document.body && document.body.classList.contains('modal-open')) return true;
029201:         return SUPPRESSION_SELECTORS.some(selector => {
029202:             let nodes;
029203:             try { nodes = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(selector)); } catch (err) { return false; }
029204:             return nodes.some(el => {
029205:                 if (!el || el.closest(`#${SCRIPT.controlId}`) || el.closest(`#${SCRIPT.panelId}`)) return false;
029206:                 if (!isVisible(el)) return false;
029207:                 const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
029208:                 return (rect.width * rect.height) > 1200;
029209:             });
029210:         });
029211:     }
029212:

029214:         const control = document.getElementById(SCRIPT.controlId);
029215:         if (!control) return;
029216:         control.classList.toggle('mcms-hidden-by-menu', shouldSuppressControl());
029217:     }

030877:                 target.closest?.(`#${SCRIPT.missionRequirementsPanelId}`)
030878:             )

030882:             for (const className of target.classList) {

030887:         let elementCount = 0;
030888:         for (const collection of [mutation.addedNodes, mutation.removedNodes]) {
030889:             if (!collection?.length) continue;
030890:             for (const node of collection) {
030891:                 if (!node || node.nodeType !== 1) continue;
030892:                 elementCount += 1;
030893:                 if (!(node.matches?.(toolkitSelector) || node.querySelector?.(toolkitSelector))) return false;
030894:             }
030895:         }
030896:         return elementCount > 0;
030897:     }

030910:     function mutationTouchesSelector(mutation, selector) {
030911:         const target = mutation?.target;
030912:         if (target?.nodeType === 1 && (target.matches?.(selector) || target.closest?.(selector))) return true;
030913:         for (const collection of [mutation?.addedNodes, mutation?.removedNodes]) {
030914:             if (!collection?.length) continue;
030915:             for (const node of collection) {
030916:                 if (!node || node.nodeType !== 1) continue;
030917:                 if (node.matches?.(selector) || node.querySelector?.(selector)) return true;
030918:             }
030919:         }
030920:         return false;
030921:     }

031023:     function pruneRuntimeCaches(now = Date.now()) {
031024:         for (const [missionId, panel] of missionPanelCache.entries()) {
031025:             if (!panel?.isConnected) missionPanelCache.delete(missionId);
031026:         }
031027:         for (const [missionId, cached] of missionSnapshotCache.entries()) {
031028:             if (liveMissionSnapshots.has(missionId)) continue;
031029:             if (now - Number(cached?.lastUsed || now) > MISSION_CACHE_RETENTION_MS) missionSnapshotCache.delete(missionId);
031030:         }
031031:         for (const missionId of missionOverlayVersions.keys()) {
031032:             if (!missionOverlayData.has(missionId)) missionOverlayVersions.delete(missionId);
031033:         }
031034:         for (const [name, cached] of markerRegistryCache.entries()) {
031035:             if (now - Number(cached?.createdAt || now) > RUNTIME_CACHE_PRUNE_MS) markerRegistryCache.delete(name);
031036:         }
031037:         for (const [missionId, cached] of criticalMissionStableCache.entries()) {
031038:             if (liveMissionSnapshots.has(missionId)) continue;
031039:             if (now - Number(cached?.lastSeen || now) > MISSION_CACHE_RETENTION_MS) criticalMissionStableCache.delete(missionId);
031040:         }
031041:         for (const [key, cached] of resourceGapAnalysisCache.entries()) {
031042:             if (now - Number(cached?.createdAt || now) > Math.max(2 * RESOURCE_GAP_REFRESH_MS, RUNTIME_CACHE_PRUNE_MS)) resourceGapAnalysisCache.delete(key);
031043:         }
031044:         if (resourceGapAnalysisCache.size > 180) {
031045:             const ordered = Array.from(resourceGapAnalysisCache.entries()).sort((a, b) => Number(a[1]?.createdAt || 0) - Number(b[1]?.createdAt || 0));
031046:             for (const [key] of ordered.slice(0, resourceGapAnalysisCache.size - 180)) resourceGapAnalysisCache.delete(key);
031047:         }
031048:         const currentVehicleLayers = new Set(getVehicleMarkerLayers());
031049:         const currentBuildingLayers = new Set(getBuildingMarkerLayers());
031050:         for (const layer of Array.from(economyHiddenVehicleLayers)) {
031051:             if (!layer || (!layer._map && !currentVehicleLayers.has(layer))) economyHiddenVehicleLayers.delete(layer);
031052:         }
031053:         for (const layer of Array.from(economyHiddenBuildingLayers)) {
031054:             if (!layer || (!layer._map && !currentBuildingLayers.has(layer))) economyHiddenBuildingLayers.delete(layer);
031055:         }
031056:         if (!state.resourceGap.enabled) {
031057:             resourceGapAnalysisCache.clear();
031058:             resourceGapVehicleContextCache = { key: '', createdAt: 0, available: [], byToken: new Map() };
031059:         }
031060:         if (!state.heatmap.enabled && heatmapSourceCache.points.length) heatmapSourceCache = { key: '', createdAt: 0, points: [] };
031061:     }

031064:         const initiallyInContext = isAllianceBuildingsContext();
031065:         const enabled = state.allianceBuildingsMap !== false;
031066:         let renderTimer = null;

031082:             runtimeSetTimeout(renderWhenRelevant, 1200);
031083:             const pageObserver = runtimeTrackObserver(new MutationObserver(mutations => {
031084:                 if (!mutations.some(mutation => mutation.addedNodes?.length || mutation.removedNodes?.length)) return;
031085:                 runtimeClearTimeout(renderTimer);
031086:                 renderTimer = runtimeSetTimeout(() => {
031087:                     renderTimer = null;
031088:                     renderWhenRelevant();
031089:                 }, 0);
031090:             }));
031091:             pageObserver.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });
031092:         }
031093:         runtimeListen(document, 'click', event => {
031094:             const button = closestEventTarget(event, '[data-mcms-alliance-map-toggle]');
031095:             if (!button) return;
031096:             event.preventDefault();

031099:             saveState();
031100:             button.disabled = true;
031101:             button.textContent = 'Reloading…';
031102:             runtimeSetTimeout(() => location.reload(), 120);
031103:         }, true);
031104:         runtimeOnCleanup(() => {
031105:             document.getElementById(ALLIANCE_BUILDINGS_MAP_NOTICE_ID)?.remove();
031106:             document.querySelectorAll('.mcms-alliance-buildings-map-column').forEach(element => element.classList.remove('mcms-alliance-buildings-map-column'));
031107:             document.querySelectorAll('.mcms-alliance-buildings-list-column').forEach(element => element.classList.remove('mcms-alliance-buildings-list-column'));
031108:             document.querySelectorAll('[data-mcms-alliance-map-column], [data-mcms-alliance-list-column]').forEach(element => {
031109:                 element.removeAttribute('data-mcms-alliance-map-column');
031110:                 element.removeAttribute('data-mcms-alliance-list-column');
031111:             });
031112:             document.documentElement?.removeAttribute('data-mcms-alliance-buildings-page');
031113:         });
031114:         return initiallyInContext && !enabled;
031115:     }

031137:     async function runDeferredOperationalStartup() {
031138:         if (operationalStartupStarted || runtime.destroyed) return;
031139:         const operationalPerformanceStartedAt = startupClock();

031141:             runtimeSetTimeout(() => scheduleDeferredOperationalStartup(0), 1000);

031153:         try {
031154:             if (vehicleDataNeeded()) await refreshPersonalVehicleData(true);
031155:         } finally {

031163:         if (state.transportWatcher) scheduleTransportWatcherRefresh(220);
031164:         if (state.resourceGap.enabled) scheduleResourceGapRefresh(260);
031165:         if (state.unitCommitment) scheduleUnitCommitmentRefresh(300);
031166:         if (state.allianceCredits) scheduleAllianceCreditRefresh(320);
031167:         if (state.missionAge) scheduleMissionAgeRefresh(340);

031170:         if (state.majorIncidentFeed.enabled) scheduleMajorIncidentFeedRender(120);
031171:         scheduleEnabledMapRefreshes({ includeSnapshots: false, positionPanel: false, mapOnly: true });
031172:         recordStartupMetric('operationalStartupMs', operationalPerformanceStartedAt, { operationalStartupComplete: true });
031173: 
031174:     }

031176:     function scheduleDeferredOperationalStartup(delay = STARTUP_OPERATIONAL_DELAY_MS) {
031177:         if (operationalStartupStarted || runtime.destroyed) return;
031178:         runtimeSetTimeout(() => runtimeRunWhenIdle(() => {
031179:             runDeferredOperationalStartup().catch(err => {
031180:                 operationalStartupComplete = true;
031181:                 startupDataPassActive = false;
031182:                 console.debug(`[${SCRIPT.name}] Deferred startup recovered after an operational initialisation error.`, err);
031183:                 connectMainMutationObserver();
031184:             });
031185:         }, STARTUP_IDLE_TIMEOUT_MS), Math.max(0, Number(delay) || 0));
031186:     }

031190:     const AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_MISSION_ROOT_SELECTOR = '#lightbox_box, #lightbox, .lightbox_content, .modal.show, .modal.in, .modal-content, [role="dialog"], .ui-dialog-content, .ui-dialog';
031191:     const AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_MAX_REQUESTS = 50;

031209:     function autoLoadAllVehiclesLinkInfo(link) {
031210:         if (!link || link.nodeType !== 1 || !link.matches?.(AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_SELECTOR)) return null;
031211:         let url;
031212:         try { url = new URL(link.getAttribute('href') || link.href, location.href); } catch (err) { return null; }
031213:         if (url.origin !== location.origin) return null;
031214:         const match = url.pathname.match(/^\/missions\/(\d+)\/missing_vehicles\/?$/u);
031215:         if (!match) return null;
031216:         const rawOffset = url.searchParams.get('offset_page');
031217:         const offsetPage = Number.isFinite(Number(rawOffset)) ? Math.max(0, Number(rawOffset)) : 0;
031218:         return {
031219:             missionId: match[1],
031220:             offsetPage,
031221:             signature: `${match[1]}:${offsetPage}:${url.pathname}${url.search}`,
031222:             href: url.href
031223:         };
031224:     }
031225: 
031226:     function autoLoadAllVehiclesElementVisible(element) {
031227:         if (!element?.isConnected || element.hidden || element.getAttribute?.('aria-hidden') === 'true') return false;
031228:         if (element.matches?.(':disabled, .disabled, [aria-disabled="true"]')) return false;
031229:         try {
031230:             const style = pageWindow.getComputedStyle?.(element);
031231:             if (style?.display === 'none' || style?.visibility === 'hidden' || style?.visibility === 'collapse' || style?.pointerEvents === 'none' || Number(style?.opacity) === 0) return false;
031232:             const rect = element.getBoundingClientRect?.();
031233:             return !rect || (rect.width > 1 && rect.height > 1);
031234:         } catch (err) {
031235:             return true;
031236:         }
031237:     }

031239:     function autoLoadAllVehiclesResolveMissionRoot(link) {
031240:         return link.closest?.(AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_MISSION_ROOT_SELECTOR) || link.parentElement || document.body;
031241:     }

031243:     function autoLoadAllVehiclesCandidateLinks() {
031244:         if (!state.autoLoadAllVehicles) return [];
031245:         const queryRoot = autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot?.isConnected && autoLoadAllVehiclesElementVisible(autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot)
031246:             ? autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot
031247:             : document;
031248:         return Array.from(queryRoot.querySelectorAll(AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_SELECTOR))
031249:             .reverse()
031250:             .map(link => ({ link, info: autoLoadAllVehiclesLinkInfo(link) }))
031251:             .filter(candidate => Boolean(candidate.info));
031252:     }

031273:         autoLoadAllVehiclesActiveLink = null;
031274:         autoLoadAllVehiclesActiveSignature = '';
031275:         if (schedule && state.autoLoadAllVehicles) scheduleAutoLoadAllVehiclesScan(AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_SETTLE_MS);
031276:     }

031278:     function resetAutoLoadAllVehiclesMission() {
031279:         releaseAutoLoadAllVehiclesRequest({ schedule: false });
031280:         disconnectAutoLoadAllVehiclesRootObserver();
031281:         autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionId = null;
031282:         autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot = null;
031283:         autoLoadAllVehiclesRequestCount = 0;
031284:         autoLoadAllVehiclesHiddenRetryCount = 0;
031285:         autoLoadAllVehiclesRequestedPages.clear();

031288:     function observeAutoLoadAllVehiclesRoot(root) {
031289:         disconnectAutoLoadAllVehiclesRootObserver();
031290:         if (!root || root === document.body) return;
031291:         const observer = runtimeTrackObserver(new MutationObserver(() => {
031292:             if (!state.autoLoadAllVehicles) return;
031293:             if (!root.isConnected || !autoLoadAllVehiclesElementVisible(root)) {
031294:                 resetAutoLoadAllVehiclesMission();
031295:                 return;
031296:             }
031297:             scheduleAutoLoadAllVehiclesScan(AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_SETTLE_MS);
031298:         }));
031299:         observer.observe(root, {
031300:             attributes: true,
031301:             attributeFilter: ['class', 'style', 'hidden', 'aria-hidden']
031302:         });
031303:         autoLoadAllVehiclesRootObserver = observer;
031304:     }
031305: 
031306:     function observeAutoLoadAllVehiclesLink(link) {
031307:         disconnectAutoLoadAllVehiclesLinkObserver();
031308:         if (!link) return;
031309:         const observer = runtimeTrackObserver(new MutationObserver(() => {
031310:             if (!state.autoLoadAllVehicles) return;
031311:             const info = autoLoadAllVehiclesLinkInfo(link);
031312:             const changed = Boolean(info && info.signature !== autoLoadAllVehiclesActiveSignature);
031313:             if (!link.isConnected || !info || !autoLoadAllVehiclesElementVisible(link) || changed) {
031314:                 releaseAutoLoadAllVehiclesRequest({ schedule: true });
031315:             }
031316:         }));
031317:         observer.observe(link, {
031318:             attributes: true,
031319:             attributeFilter: ['href', 'class', 'style', 'hidden', 'aria-hidden', 'aria-disabled']
031320:         });
031321:         autoLoadAllVehiclesLinkObserver = observer;
031322:     }

031324:     function scheduleAutoLoadAllVehiclesScan(delay = 0) {
031325:         if (!state.autoLoadAllVehicles || runtime.destroyed) return;
031326:         runtimeClearTimeout(autoLoadAllVehiclesScanTimer);
031327:         autoLoadAllVehiclesScanTimer = runtimeSetTimeout(() => {
031328:             autoLoadAllVehiclesScanTimer = null;
031329:             scanAutoLoadAllVehicles();
031330:         }, Math.max(0, Number(delay) || 0));
031331:     }
031332: 
031333:     function scanAutoLoadAllVehicles() {
031334:         if (!state.autoLoadAllVehicles || runtime.destroyed || autoLoadAllVehiclesInFlight) return false;
031335:         const candidates = autoLoadAllVehiclesCandidateLinks();
031336:         if (!candidates.length) {
031337:             autoLoadAllVehiclesHiddenRetryCount = 0;
031338:             if (autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot && (!autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot.isConnected || !autoLoadAllVehiclesElementVisible(autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot))) {
031339:                 resetAutoLoadAllVehiclesMission();
031340:             }
031341:             return false;
031342:         }
031343:         const visibleCandidates = candidates.filter(candidate => autoLoadAllVehiclesElementVisible(candidate.link));
031344:         if (!visibleCandidates.length) {
031345:             if (autoLoadAllVehiclesHiddenRetryCount < AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_HIDDEN_RETRIES) {
031346:                 autoLoadAllVehiclesHiddenRetryCount += 1;
031347:                 scheduleAutoLoadAllVehiclesScan(AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_SETTLE_MS);
031348:             }
031349:             return false;
031350:         }
031351:         autoLoadAllVehiclesHiddenRetryCount = 0;
031352:         const candidate = visibleCandidates.find(item => item.info.missionId !== autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionId || !autoLoadAllVehiclesRequestedPages.has(item.info.signature)) || visibleCandidates[0];
031353:         const { link, info } = candidate;
031354:         const missionRoot = autoLoadAllVehiclesResolveMissionRoot(link);
031355:         if (info.missionId !== autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionId || missionRoot !== autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot) {
031356:             resetAutoLoadAllVehiclesMission();
031357:             autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionId = info.missionId;
031358:             autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot = missionRoot;
031359:             observeAutoLoadAllVehiclesRoot(missionRoot);
031360:         }
031361:         if (autoLoadAllVehiclesRequestedPages.has(info.signature)) return false;
031362:         if (autoLoadAllVehiclesRequestCount >= AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_MAX_REQUESTS) {
031363:             console.warn(`[${SCRIPT.name}] Auto-load all vehicles stopped after ${AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_MAX_REQUESTS} requests for mission ${info.missionId}.`);
031364:             return false;
031365:         }
031366:         autoLoadAllVehiclesRequestedPages.add(info.signature);
031367:         autoLoadAllVehiclesRequestCount += 1;
031368:         autoLoadAllVehiclesInFlight = true;
031369:         autoLoadAllVehiclesActiveLink = link;
031370:         autoLoadAllVehiclesActiveSignature = info.signature;
031371:         link.dataset.mcmsAutoLoadRequested = 'true';
031372:         observeAutoLoadAllVehiclesLink(link);
031373:         try {
031374:             link.click();
031375:         } catch (err) {
031376:             autoLoadAllVehiclesRequestedPages.delete(info.signature);
031377:             releaseAutoLoadAllVehiclesRequest({ schedule: false });
031378:             console.warn(`[${SCRIPT.name}] Auto-load all vehicles could not activate MissionChief's native control.`, err);
031379:             return false;
031380:         }
031381:         clearAutoLoadAllVehiclesReleaseTimer();
031382:         autoLoadAllVehiclesReleaseTimer = runtimeSetTimeout(() => {
031383:             autoLoadAllVehiclesReleaseTimer = null;
031384:             releaseAutoLoadAllVehiclesRequest({ schedule: true });
031385:         }, AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_TIMEOUT_MS);
031386:         return true;
031387:     }
031388: 
031389:     function autoLoadAllVehiclesMutationRelevant(mutation) {
031390:         if (mutation.type !== 'childList') return false;
031391:         const nodes = [...Array.from(mutation.addedNodes || []), ...Array.from(mutation.removedNodes || [])];
031392:         return nodes.some(node => {
031393:             if (!node || node.nodeType !== 1) return false;
031394:             if (autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot && (node === autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot || node.contains?.(autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot))) return true;
031395:             return Boolean(
031396:                 node.matches?.(AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_SELECTOR) ||
031397:                 node.querySelector?.(AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_SELECTOR) ||
031398:                 node.matches?.(AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_MISSION_ROOT_SELECTOR) ||
031399:                 node.querySelector?.(AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_MISSION_ROOT_SELECTOR)
031400:             );
031401:         });
031402:     }

031412:     function installAutoLoadAllVehicles() {
031413:         if (!state.autoLoadAllVehicles || runtime.destroyed) {
031414:             stopAutoLoadAllVehicles();
031415:             return false;
031416:         }
031417:         if (!document.body) {
031418:             runtimeListen(document, 'DOMContentLoaded', installAutoLoadAllVehicles, { once: true });
031419:             return false;
031420:         }
031421:         if (!autoLoadAllVehiclesObserver) {
031422:             const observer = runtimeTrackObserver(new MutationObserver(mutations => {
031423:                 if (!state.autoLoadAllVehicles) return;
031424:                 if (autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot && !autoLoadAllVehiclesMissionRoot.isConnected) {
031425:                     resetAutoLoadAllVehiclesMission();
031426:                 }
031427:                 if (autoLoadAllVehiclesActiveLink && !autoLoadAllVehiclesActiveLink.isConnected) {
031428:                     releaseAutoLoadAllVehiclesRequest({ schedule: false });
031429:                 }
031430:                 if (mutations.some(autoLoadAllVehiclesMutationRelevant)) scheduleAutoLoadAllVehiclesScan(AUTO_LOAD_ALL_VEHICLES_SETTLE_MS);
031431:             }));
031432:             observer.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });
031433:             autoLoadAllVehiclesObserver = observer;
031434:         }
031435:         scheduleAutoLoadAllVehiclesScan(0);
031436:         return true;
031437:     }

031440:     function startBootAttemptCoordinator(bootPerformanceStartedAt) {
031441:         let attempts = 0;
031442:         const runBootAttempt = () => {
031443:             attempts += 1;
031444:             installMissionMarkerAddHook();
031445:             installRadioMessageHook();
031446:             installCreditsUpdateHook();
031447:             observeCreditValue();
031448:             const ready = ensureUi();
031449:             const mapReady = Boolean(getLargestLeafletMap());
031450:             if (ready && (mapReady || attempts >= 12)) {
031451:                 recordStartupMetric('coreUiReadyMs', bootPerformanceStartedAt, { bootAttempts: attempts });
031452:                 scheduleMarkerStateSync(0, false);
031453:                 scheduleDeferredOperationalStartup();
031454:                 scheduleVersionStatusCheck(VERSION_STATUS.bootDelayMs, false);
031455:                 runtimeSetTimeout(() => runtimeRunWhenIdle(connectMainMutationObserver, STARTUP_OBSERVER_DELAY_MS), STARTUP_OBSERVER_DELAY_MS);
031456:                 return;
031457:             }
031458:             if (attempts >= 90 || runtime.destroyed) return;
031459:             const delay = attempts < 12 ? 350 : attempts < 30 ? 700 : 1400;
031460:             runtimeSetTimeout(runBootAttempt, delay);
031461:         };
031462:         runtimeSetTimeout(runBootAttempt, 250);
031463:     }
031464: 
031465:     function boot() {
031466:         if (runtime.destroyed || bootStarted) return;
031467:         bootStarted = true;
031468:         bootStartedAt = Date.now();
031469:         const bootPerformanceStartedAt = startupClock();
031470:         applyRootAttributes();
031471:         if (installAllianceBuildingsPageOptimisation()) return;
031472:         createCleanExit();
031473:         if (state.autoLoadAllVehicles) installAutoLoadAllVehicles();
031474:         installMissionMarkerAddHook();
031475:         installRadioMessageHook();
031476:         lastObservedCredits = readCurrentCreditTotal();
031477:         installCreditsUpdateHook();
031478:         observeCreditValue();
031479:         installMissionRequirementsWindows();
031480:         installCustomVehicleBadges();
031481:         startBootAttemptCoordinator(bootPerformanceStartedAt);
031482:         const observer = runtimeTrackObserver(new MutationObserver(mutations => {
031483:             if (state.economyMode && economyMapMoving) {
031484:                 economyDeferredDomMutation = true;
031485:                 return;
031486:             }
031487:             let externalMutationFound = false;
031488:             let addedLeafletMarker = false;
031489:             let missionChanged = false;
031490:             let layoutChanged = false;
031491:             let toolkitUiRemoved = false;
031492:             for (const mutation of mutations) {
031493:                 if (mutationBelongsToToolkit(mutation)) continue;
031494:                 externalMutationFound = true;
031495:                 if (!addedLeafletMarker && mutationAddsLeafletMarkerIcon(mutation)) {
031496:                     addedLeafletMarker = true;
031497:                     missionChanged = true;
031498:                 }
031499:                 if (!missionChanged && mutationAffectsMissionData(mutation)) missionChanged = true;
031500:                 if (!layoutChanged && mutationAffectsMapLayout(mutation)) layoutChanged = true;
031501:                 if (!toolkitUiRemoved && mutationRemovesToolkitUi(mutation)) toolkitUiRemoved = true;
031502:                 if (addedLeafletMarker && missionChanged && layoutChanged && toolkitUiRemoved) break;
031503:             }
031504:             if (!externalMutationFound) return;
031505:             missionChanged ||= addedLeafletMarker;
031506:             if (!missionChanged && !layoutChanged && !toolkitUiRemoved) return;
031507:             if (addedLeafletMarker) {
031508:                 invalidateMarkerRegistryCaches('all');
031509:                 scheduleMarkerStateSync(0, false);
031510:                 if (!state.visibility.buildings) scheduleMarkerStateSync(180, true);
031511:             }
031512:             if (layoutChanged) invalidateMapElementCache();
031513:             if (document.hidden || dragState || (state.economyMode && economyMapMoving)) return;
031514:             runtimeClearTimeout(mutationTimer);
031515:             const startupSettling = bootStartedAt > 0 && Date.now() - bootStartedAt < STARTUP_SETTLE_WINDOW_MS;
031516:             const mutationDelay = startupSettling
031517:                 ? STARTUP_MUTATION_DEBOUNCE_MS
031518:                 : (state.economyMode ? Math.max(320, DOM_REFRESH_DEBOUNCE_MS) : DOM_REFRESH_DEBOUNCE_MS);
031519:             mutationTimer = runtimeSetTimeout(() => {
031520:                 if (dragState || document.hidden || runtime.destroyed || (state.economyMode && economyMapMoving)) return;
031521:                 const panelMissing = settingsPanelActivated && !document.getElementById(SCRIPT.panelId);
031522:                 const mapElement = getLargestLeafletMap();
031523:                 const controlMissing = Boolean(mapElement && !document.getElementById(SCRIPT.controlId));
031524:                 if (toolkitUiRemoved || panelMissing || controlMissing) ensureUi();
031525:                 if (mainMutationObserverFallbackActive && (mapElement || document.querySelector('#missions, #mission_list, .missions-panel, .mission-list'))) {
031526:                     connectMainMutationObserver();
031527:                 }
031528:                 if (layoutChanged) {
031529:                     refreshSuppression();
031530:                     fitControlToMap();
031531:                     schedulePanelPosition(true, 50);
031532:                     scheduleCriticalDrawerDock(60);
031533:                 }
031534:                 if (missionChanged) {
031535:                     scheduleEnabledMapRefreshes({ includeSnapshots: missionSnapshotsNeeded(), positionPanel: false });
031536:                     scheduleMissionRequirementsScan(35);
031537:                 }
031538:             }, mutationDelay);
031539:         }));
031540:         mainMutationObserver = observer;
031541:         runtimeListen(document, 'keydown', handleKeyboard);
031542:         runtimeListen(document, 'pointerover', handleMissionInspectorPointerOver, true);
031543:         runtimeListen(document, 'pointermove', handleMissionInspectorPointerMove, true);
031544:         runtimeListen(document, 'pointerout', handleMissionInspectorPointerOut, true);
031545:         runtimeListen(document, 'pointerdown', () => unlockPayoutAudio(), { once: true, capture: true });
031546:         runtimeListen(document, 'click', event => {
031547:             runtimeSetTimeout(refreshSuppression, 0);
031548:             if (suppressNextOutsideClick) {
031549:                 event.preventDefault();
031550:                 event.stopPropagation();
031551:                 suppressNextOutsideClick = false;
031552:                 return;
031553:             }
031554:             const control = document.getElementById(SCRIPT.controlId);
031555:             const panel = document.getElementById(SCRIPT.panelId);
031556:             if (!panel || !panel.classList.contains('mcms-open')) return;
031557:             if (control && control.contains(event.target)) return;
031558:             if (panel.contains(event.target)) return;
031559:             closePanel();
031560:         }, true);
031561:         runtimeListen(pageWindow, 'resize', () => {
031562:             invalidateMapElementCache();
031563:             applyRootAttributes();
031564:             refreshTabletModeUi();
031565:             scheduleTabletLayoutRefresh(20);
031566:             const payoutOverlay = document.getElementById(SCRIPT.payoutFlashId);
031567:             if (payoutOverlay?.classList.contains('mcms-payout-active')) positionPayoutFlashOverlay(payoutOverlay);
031568:             if (dragState) return;
031569:             refreshSuppression();
031570:             fitControlToMap();
031571:             schedulePanelPosition(true, 40);
031572:             scheduleCriticalDrawerDock(30);
031573:             scheduleEnabledMapRefreshes({ includeSnapshots: false, positionPanel: false, mapOnly: true });
031574:             scheduleMajorIncidentFeedLayout();
031575:         });
031576:         runtimeListen(pageWindow, 'scroll', scheduleMajorIncidentFeedLayout, { passive: true });

029746:     function buildThemeOptions(selected) {
029747:         return THEME_ORDER.map(key => `<option value="${key}" ${key === selected ? 'selected' : ''}>${THEMES[key].full}</option>`).join('');
029748:     }
029749: 
029750:     function makeToggleButton(key, icon, label, title) {
029751:         return `
029752:             <button class="mcms-toggle-btn" type="button" data-toggle="${key}" title="${escapeHtml(title || label)}">
029753:                 <span class="mcms-iconbox">${icon}</span>
029754:                 <span class="mcms-text">
029755:                     <span class="mcms-label">${escapeHtml(label)}</span>
029756:                     <span class="mcms-pill">OFF</span>
029757:                 </span>
029758:             </button>
029759:         `;
029760:     }

029182:     function isNightNow(start, end) {
029183:         const now = new Date();
029184:         const current = now.getHours() * 60 + now.getMinutes();
029185:         const startMin = parseTime(start, 19 * 60);
029186:         const endMin = parseTime(end, 7 * 60);
029187:         if (startMin === endMin) return false;
029188:         if (startMin < endMin) return current >= startMin && current < endMin;

029171:     function runAutoNight(force = false) {
029172:         if (!state.autoNight.enabled) return;
029173:         const bucket = isNightNow(state.autoNight.nightStart, state.autoNight.dayStart) ? 'night' : 'day';
029174:         if (!force && state.autoNight.lastBucket === bucket) return;
029175:         state.autoNight.lastBucket = bucket;
029176:         state.theme = bucket === 'night' ? normaliseTheme(state.autoNight.nightTheme) : normaliseTheme(state.autoNight.dayTheme);
029177:         saveState();
029178:         applyRootAttributes();
029179:         updateUI();
029180:     }

029186:         const endMin = parseTime(end, 7 * 60);
029187:         if (startMin === endMin) return false;

029788:     function versionStatusCompare(left, right) { const a = versionStatusParse(left); const b = versionStatusParse(right); if (!a || !b) return null; for (let index = 0; index < 3; index += 1) { if (a[index] !== b[index]) return a[index] > b[index] ? 1 : -1; } return 0; }
029789:     function versionStatusUrl(value, kind, version) { let url; try { url = new URL(String(value || '')); } catch (err) { throw new Error(`Invalid ${kind} URL.`); } if (url.protocol !== 'https:') throw new Error(`${kind} URL must use HTTPS.`); if (kind === 'release') { const expected = `/Conroy1988/missionchief-toolkit-assets/releases/tag/v${version}`; if (url.hostname !== 'github.com' || url.pathname !== expected) throw new Error('Release URL is not canonical.'); } else if (url.hostname !== 'update.greasyfork.org' || !/^\/scripts\/586018\/.+\.user\.js$/u.test(url.pathname)) throw new Error('Update URL is not canonical.'); return url.href; }
029790:     function versionStatusValidateManifest(payload) { if (!payload || typeof payload !== 'object' || Array.isArray(payload)) throw new Error('Version manifest is not an object.'); if (Number(payload.schemaVersion) !== 1 || payload.channel !== 'stable') throw new Error('Version manifest channel is invalid.'); const version = String(payload.version || '').trim(); if (!versionStatusParse(version)) throw new Error('Version manifest does not contain a stable semantic version.'); return { schemaVersion: 1, channel: 'stable', version, releaseNotesUrl: versionStatusUrl(payload.releaseNotesUrl, 'release', version), updateUrl: versionStatusUrl(payload.updateUrl, 'update', version), publishedAt: String(payload.publishedAt || '') }; }
